        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

# Use-after-Free in FileSystemChooseEntryFunction::FilesSelected



<span class="line"><!----># Use-after-Free in FileSystemChooseEntryFunction::FilesSelected<!----></span>



<br>





## Root Cause and some notes



<span class="line"><!---->## Root Cause and some notes<!----></span>



<br>





The `web_contents` is posted to a separate sequence[0] and `web_contents` may be destroyed in UI by the time it runs,When it post webcontents back[1] from a seperate sequence and use it in[2],UAF happens.



<span class="line"><!---->The `web_contents` is posted to a separate sequence[0] and `web_contents` may be destroyed in UI by the time it runs,When it post webcontents back[1] from a seperate sequence and use it in[2],UAF happens.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[0]



<span class="line"><!---->[0]<!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:extensions/browser/api/file_system/file_system_api.cc;l=537?q=file_system_api

This bug requires manual review: M93's targeted beta branch promotion date has already passed, so this requires manual review



<span class="line"><!---->This bug requires manual review: M93's targeted beta branch promotion date has already passed, so this requires manual review<!----></span>



<br>





Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?



<span class="line"><!---->1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?<!----></span>



<br>





- Chrome: 



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome: <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src.git/+/main/docs/process/merge_request.md#when-to-request-a-merge



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src.git/+/main/docs/process/merge_request.md#when-to-request-a-merge"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src.git/+/main/docs/process/merge_request.md#when-to-request-a-merge<!----></a>



<br>





- Chrome OS: 



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome OS: <!----></span>





https://goto.google.com/cros-release-branch-merge-guidelines



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://goto.google.com/cros-release-branch-merge-guidelines"><!---->https://goto.google.com/cros-release-branch-merge-guidelines<!----></a>



<br>





2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?



<span class="line"><!---->3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?<!----></span>



<br>





4. Does this change need to be merged into other active release branches (M-1, M+1)?



<span class="line"><!---->4. Does this change need to be merged into other active release branches (M-1, M+1)?<!----></span>



<br>





5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?



<span class="line"><!---->5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?<!----></span>



<br>





6. Is this a new feature?



<span class="line"><!---->6. Is this a new feature?<!----></span>



<br>





7. If it is a new feature, is it behind a flag using finch?



<span class="line"><!---->7. If it is a new feature, is it behind a flag using finch?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Chrome OS Only:



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome OS Only:<!----></span>



<br>





8. Was the change reviewed and approved by the Eng Prod Representative? See Eng Prod ownership by component: 



<span class="line"><!---->8. Was the change reviewed and approved by the Eng Prod Representative? See Eng Prod ownership by component: <!----></span>





http://go/cros-engprodcomponents

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
